If you are the first one to join, you would be assigned the drawer for the first round. You would be given a random word. Alternatively, you can tap \"Pick Color\" to bring up the large color wheel. \r\n\r\nIf you made a mistake, you can say \"Erase Last Stroke\" or press right hand controller grab button.
